Fuzhou

Gambling Houses are Extremely Popular

No Less Than a Dozen in the Entire City

All Opened by Taiwanese People

Fuzhou Correspondence: The trend of gambling houses has been extremely popular in Minyuan recently. In total, there are no less than a dozen in the entire city, all opened by Japanese Taiwanese. Most of them are open three times a day, at 12:00 noon, 5:00 pm, and 10:00 pm. Some of them are open twice a day, at noon and in the evening, or in the evening and at night. Each round has hundreds of people betting, and thousands of people betting a lot, especially in the evening. Among them, the Xingji Foreign Firm in Huaidefang, the Xinlong Foreign Firm in Wenzaoshan, and the Showa Foreign Firm in Nanmendou have the largest venues. Every time the round is opened, the bettors fill the road, and traffic is cut off. There are also a dozen Taiwanese people carrying pistols to protect the venue, and their fierce arrogance is unbearable. It has been found that large venues can make a profit of three or four hundred yuan a day, and small venues can also make a profit of one or two hundred yuan. Men and women in the middle and lower classes of society lose their minds due to gambling and seek help from gods and Buddhas everywhere. No matter what kind of desolate ancient temple, people pray for dreams and make words. Even places like Jigao Lane (mountain name), the execution ground outside the West Gate, and the Maze Cave, the demon lair of Wushi Mountain, which timid people dare not go to on weekdays, are now visited by hundreds of people every night to pray for dreams. Men and women are mixed together, and their ugly behavior is fully exposed. Every evening, no matter on the main streets or alleys, whenever you see pedestrians in groups of three or five, what they talk about is nothing but gambling houses. Recently, women have committed suicide almost every day because they lost gambling and were unable to pay off their debts or were afraid of being questioned by their families. Public opinion is deeply dissatisfied with the silence and indulgence of the officials. The County Party Affairs Guidance Committee and the New Life Movement Promotion Association have repeatedly petitioned the government to find a way to prohibit it. The Nanchang Commander-in-Chief’s Office also issued a notice to Fujian to investigate and ban it based on reports from various sources. For this reason, the provincial government has specially formulated the Interim Regulations on Punishing Special Gambling in the hope of eliminating the gambling trend. It stipulates that those who engage in opening gambling houses shall be sentenced to death or imprisonment for more than ten years and may be fined up to 8,000 yuan. Those who work in gambling houses shall be sentenced to imprisonment for more than three years and less than seven years and may be fined up to 5,000 yuan. Those who gather crowds to resist officers and soldiers by opening gambling houses or seek shelter from foreigners shall be sentenced to death. Military police and officials who harbor and protect gambling houses shall also be sentenced to death. The regulations were promulgated and implemented on the 2nd. From the 3rd, the Public Security Bureau has dispatched a large number of detectives and arrested more than a dozen Chinese partners used in the gambling houses, and decided to severely punish them. The rest are still being investigated. As for how to ban and close the gambling houses opened by Taiwanese people in order to fundamentally eliminate the gambling trend, it is still under consideration and negotiation. (September 3rd)

Henan Province

Run on the Agricultural and Industrial Bank

——The Situation Has Gradually Stabilized After the Authorities Took Measures to Maintain It——

Kaifeng Correspondence: Since the Xin Chang and Tong He Yu silver shops went bankrupt one after another in Bianyuan last year, a tight turnover situation has been presented. This year, the Fuli, Zheng Chang, and Hong Feng shops have also closed down one after another, causing the citizens to feel uneasy again. The pain of the paper money issued by the Yuquan Official Silver Shop, the Henan Provincial Bank, and the Northwest Bank since the Republic of China being equal to waste paper has long given the general public a bad impression. However, the Henan Provincial Agricultural and Industrial Bank suddenly experienced a run on the bank on the 4th and 5th (yesterday and today). The following is a record of what happened:

The Henan Provincial Agricultural and Industrial Bank is a provincial bank in nature and is the economic center of the entire Henan Province. It has issued a large number of banknotes in various denominations, including 10 cents, 20 cents, 50 cents, 1 yuan, 5 yuan, and 10 yuan, which are commonly used throughout Henan Province. According to the official announcement, the cash reserve checked by the supervisor this month was more than 1.1 million yuan, the security reserve was more than 660,000 yuan, plus a fund of more than 1 million yuan, which was more than sufficient to pay for the exchange of banknotes. However, Li Hanzhen, the general manager of the bank, recently resigned from his concurrent position as general manager of the Jiaozuo and Zhongfu Companies Joint Office and went to Zhangde and other places in northern Henan on the 1st to inspect the bank's affairs. Those who did not know the inside story mistakenly thought that he had resigned and left Bianjing, which led to rumors that triggered the psychology of the masses who had suffered losses repeatedly. Since the afternoon of the 4th, they have been holding their banknotes to the bank in Shanhudidian Street to cash them in. Although a lot of personnel were dispatched and the cash payment was stepped up and the business hours were extended to 8 pm, it was difficult to reverse the situation of the crowd and the run on the bank. In addition, the money changers and small merchants in the city wanted to profit from it, using language to scare and buy at low prices, and the whole city fell into chaos. The market price of each yuan of Agricultural and Industrial Bank paper money went from 8,300 copper coins, to 8,000, to 7,500, to 7,000. In the back streets, some even only exchanged 4,800. In addition to dispatching military police to maintain order, the authorities decided to use political power to maintain order and economic power to maintain credit. The Central, China, Transportation, and Jincheng branches in Bianjing gathered at 9 pm to discuss the issue. Each bank, money shop, and silver firm will separately exchange Agricultural and Industrial Bank exchange coupons. The joint conference of the Chamber of Commerce also decided to maintain it uniformly. This morning, each back street money stall used the copper coins exchanged from last night to pay, and after 8 o'clock, each commercial shop in the city posted "Welcome Agricultural and Industrial Bank banknotes," and the exchange silver dollar offices all posted slogans "This shop exchanges Henan Agricultural and Industrial Bank exchange coupons". Liu Zhi and Zhang Jingping jointly issued announcements, and the bank's announcements were pasted all over the streets. Military police were standing inside and outside the bank to maintain order, and very few people went to exchange money, and the storm gradually eased. (5th)

Songjiang: A Construction Bureau Automobile Ran Over an Old Woman

Since the opening of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway, automobiles have been travelling frequently between Shanghai and Hangzhou. Yesterday (9th), an automobile of the Shanghai Construction Bureau passed through Jinshan Street, and an old woman, surnamed Qin, failed to avoid it. The automobile of the bureau drove past rapidly, and the old woman Qin was tragically run over and killed. The local sub-precinct police officer took charge of guarding the area, and reported to the county court to send a prosecutor to investigate the scene.

The Education Department Sent Personnel to Investigate the Case in Songjiang

Yu Xiufeng, sent by the Education Department, arrived in Songjiang the day before yesterday. It is heard that he is responsible for investigating the county's educational administrative affairs. He has been investigating in all directions for days, and is very meticulous. Now that the official business has been completed, he returned to the province yesterday to report on his mission.

Suzhou: Five People Injured in a Teapot Explosion

Zhao Bangxiang, the owner of Tian Heng Xiang Copper and Tin Shop, No. 110, Dongzhong Market, Qunmen, was 61 years old and from Zhenjiang. He passed away at 3:00 pm the day before yesterday (9th). His son, Deyun, hired a monk to chant sutras and burned tin ingots in a small copper basin. Until yesterday morning (10th), five people, Yuan Tong An nun Gu Yuandao, Huayue, Xinlian, Tongfa, and Yongfu An old nun Dagen and others, changed Tao Hua Bridge Yao to chant sutras. At 11:00 am, an object suddenly exploded with a loud bang in the copper basin in which the paper ingots were burned, and sparks splashed everywhere. At that time, Deyun's four-year-old son, Jin'er, was kneeling and paying respects to the deceased, and was injured in his left arm. A 16-year-old apprentice in the shop, Jin Gen, was next to him, and his left hand and lower jaw were injured. A partner also injured his shoulder, but the injuries were minor. The most pitiful ones were the old nun Dagen (58 years old) and the young nun Tongfa (12 years old), whose waists, buttocks, and thighs were injured, and their injuries were quite serious. The injured people were sent to Chide Hospital for treatment by car.

Private Counterfeit Currency Organization Busted

The Public Security Bureau's Detective Team received a confidential report on the 9th that a counterfeit currency organization was located at a certain address in Hengjie, Wuxian County. They immediately secretly dispatched detectives Fan Guangrong and Wang Xuexiang to search the area at night. They seized scattered machines such as printing presses, and 270 Shanghai China Bank double-corner banknotes that had been printed but not yet completed. They also captured criminals Hua Genpei and Chen Changlin. After leading the team, they confessed that there were manufacturing machines hidden in the Weixiaoxuan Candy Shop at the Nanxin Bridge in Jinmenkou. At midnight, they led the two criminals to the scene for investigation and seizure. All the manufacturing machines were confiscated, and a shop partner, Xu, was arrested together and taken back for interrogation.

Wuxi: Abbot of Zhifu Temple Commits Suicide by Hanging

Near Xue Sin'iang Bridge, near the south end of Nanyan City in the 8th District, there is a Zhifu Temple, co-managed by monks Yifan and Zhuxian. In normal times, the incense is very prosperous. The day before yesterday was the 30th day of the seventh lunar month, known as the birthday of the Earth Treasury, and the foolish people in the vicinity all went to chant sutras and worship Buddha, all night long. Who knew that on this day, Zhuxian suddenly hanged himself on the mezzanine of his house, kneeling with his knees on the ground. By the time he was discovered, he had already died. It is heard that the monk was only 24 years old, from the Yaojia Li family in Xialianqing. His mother is still alive, and he has four brothers. He was sent to the temple when he was young because of poverty. The reason for his suicide is unknown.

The Entire Educational Community Strives for Educational Funds

The Jiangsu Provincial Education Department ordered each county to reduce the allocation of educational funds by 60% starting this year, because the drought this year has been very severe and the income of educational funds will be affected. After receiving the order, the Wuxi County Government submitted it for discussion at the County Administrative Conference, which aroused controversy from all sides. No final decision has been made. Since the establishment of the County Treasury in this county, the teachers' salaries cannot be paid on time, which affects the county's education. A meeting of district directors was convened yesterday to decide the following: (1) Regarding the issue of reducing and discounting the payment of educational funds, the County Association and the District Associations will jointly submit a petition to the Education Department, detailing the historical background and the current situation, and the educational funds for this county should be paid in full. (2) The County Treasury has not paid the educational funds for the various schools in August, and it will be even more difficult to grasp them in the future. The Association will submit a petition to the County Government Education Bureau, requesting that the arrears for August be paid off by the 15th of this month, and that the funds for each item must be paid in full by the 15th of each month. If the goal is not achieved, we can only convene the district directors to gather at the county bureau to petition.

Chambers of Commerce in Various Counties are Allowed to be Preserved

Regarding the issue of the existence or abolition of the Chamber of Commerce, the previous Jiangsu Provincial Chamber of Commerce Joint Conference held in Wujiang once discussed it and recommended the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce Joint Committee, Yu Xiaochuan, to explain the process to the Provincial Security Department and request instructions. The day before yesterday afternoon, the chambers of commerce of various counties in southern Jiangsu continued to hold a meeting at the headquarters of the Chamber of Commerce in Suzhou. More than one hundred representatives from Zhenjiang, Suzhou, Changshu, Wuxi, Wujin, Jiangyin, Yixing, and other counties attended. The following was resolved: (1) Regarding the organization of the Chamber of Commerce, Chairman Chen has approved it. Before the establishment of the Baojia system, it is allowed to exist. Now that the drought in various counties in southern Jiangsu is very severe, the existing Chamber of Commerce should be effectively reorganized. (2) Employed group members are to be dismissed in accordance with the order. (3) The relationship between the Chamber of Commerce and local security should be reported to the provincial government by the county magistrates of each county, so that the past process can be clarified.

Changshu: Locusts Found in the Northwest Countryside

Since the beginning of summer this year, the severe drought has caused disasters, and 50% to 60% of the fields have not been transplanted with rice seedlings. Since the beginning of autumn, it has been extremely hot. Although it rained once last month, it was of no help. Fortunately, the fields along the pond were unharmed thanks to manual irrigation. Now that the county government is about to determine the autumn harvest, farmers fear that the authorities will not understand the situation and only report the condition of the fields along the pond, so they have reported the disaster situation to the various district offices. Recently, it was learned that a large number of locusts suddenly flew into the various villages in Xixushi, the fourth district, in the twilight the night before last. They came from the northeast and were numerous, covering the mountains and fields. The villagers burned incense and lit candles, and knelt down to worship. Then a part of them flew to Wang Village. Now, in addition to reporting to the county government, the district office has ordered the villagers to try their best to capture them.

Provincial Committee Secretly Investigates the Case of the Public Security Bureau Chief Being Accused

Yang Jiashu, the chief of the Meili Public Security Bureau, because he captured a local smuggler, Wang Zhicheng, also found certificates, bronze seals, guns and ammunition and all anti-animal objects in his home. Subsequently, after someone interceded, Wang Zhicheng was only presented as an ordinary smoking criminal. The head office also ordered him to be released. Later, after the people presented a provincial accusation, the head office suspended Director Yang's duties for safekeeping. However, the citizens in the countryside, because this case is of great importance, and the director of the head office, Zhou Ding, had heard about it beforehand, it is undoubtedly suspicious, and they have petitioned the province to request an investigation. After receiving the petition, the provincial government sent personnel to Changshu yesterday to secretly investigate in various places. Because their actions are extremely secretive, the content cannot be known.

Nantong: Joint Sale of Cotton from Three Counties in Shazhou

Shazhou, which is jointly administered by Nantong, Jiangyin, and Changshu counties, has a very rich cotton production. The Department of Finance sent Commissioner Zhu Yuwu to Shazhou to meet with Qian Ruchang and others, the cooperative instructors from the three counties, to discuss joint sales plans. It was decided that the weighing scale would open on the 14th.

Tangshan Agricultural Education Center Moved to Tongzhou

The Tangshan Jiangsu Provincial Farmers' Education Center was ordered to move to Nantong and renamed the Nantong Provincial People's Education Center. Wu Jianzhen, a section chief of the Education Department, and the center's director, Xi Fang, came to Tongzhou and inspected the East Park as the center's site.

The Press Celebrates Journalists' Day in Retrospect

The press in Tongyi celebrated Journalists' Day in retrospect on the 9th at the East Public Association. The meeting opened at 8:00 am and Sun Zizai and others were appointed as the presidium. The situation was extremely enthusiastic. There was a gathering for lunch. All local newspapers were closed for one day on the 10th.

Jiangyin: Department of Construction Orders County to Prohibit the Capture of Fish Fry

The head of the Provincial Fisheries Experiment Station stated that shad and knife fish are special products of the Yangtze River, and fishermen in Jiangyin and Jingjiang counties rely on them as a major source of income. However, in recent years, due to the ignorance of fishermen, they have been indiscriminately catching fish fry, resulting in a decreasing output. The spawning period for shad and knife fish is from February to May each year along the Yangtze River, and the eggs hatch into fish fry in July and August. The fishermen along the river always indiscriminately catch them with fine nets, leaving nothing behind the nets. After the fishermen catch them, they dry and sell them, but the taste is not good and the price is low. The annual catch is about 1,000 loads. Each fish fry weighs about one qian, and it can grow to one jin in two years. Counting by one thousand loads, 160,000 loads should be lost each year, worth about 2 million yuan. In other counties such as Nantong and Changshu, it is inevitable that there is such indiscriminate catching. If they are added together, the losses will be even more alarming. The head of the station specifically requested the Department of Construction to order the county magistrates of Jiang and Jing to strictly prohibit it.

Jiashan: Bandits Rob a Farmer's Home at the North Ring Bridge

Jin Huisheng, a farmer from Shaoxing, planted more than 60 mu of paddy fields at the North Ring Bridge in Gan Yao Town. His family is well-off. The day before yesterday, Huisheng went to town to buy brown rice and got 40 silver dollars. When he returned home as usual, several bandits broke into the house, twisted Jin and beat him hard, forcing him to say where he hid the money. Huisheng could not bear the pain of torture, so he told them about the money for buying rice and the original gold jewelry, etc., which were taken away to their satisfaction. In total, he lost more than fifty silver dollars.

Gaoyou: Bandits Occupy Tangjiabao

A large number of bandits have been operating in the northeast countryside of this county recently. Fearing that the army will come to suppress them, they are now breaking into smaller groups, with each group of about ten people, kidnapping in all directions. The people in the villages that have been kidnapped have fled to other places, and nine out of ten houses are empty. Tangjiabao and Daliaozai and other places near Linze are now occupied by bandits, cutting off transportation, and the situation is huge. The people in the area are terrified. The Provincial Security Team stationed in Wangying has now sent a team to Zhen Linze to act according to the opportunity to suppress them.

Jiaxing: Store Residents Campaign to Reduce Rent

Jiaxing is suffering from a severe drought, business is sluggish, and unemployment has doubled. Store residents are all feeling difficult. They are now planning to request that the rent be changed to 70% of the original payment in order to provide relief. The method is from September of this year to August of next year,

Photo of the Belgian Special Envoy and his Wife Disembarking at the North Railway Station (Photo by Wang Kai) 3

I

A public banquet was held by various groups for the Belgian Special Envoy, Baron Moncheur. The hosting organizations were the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce (Yu Zuoting, Chen Zheqing), the Chinese National Federation of Industries (Guo Shun, Hu Xiyuan), the International Problems Research Association (Liu Zhanen, Li Zhaohuan), the Bankers Association (Zhang Gongquan, Bei Songsun), and the Trade Association (Guo Bingwen, Lin Kanghou). Guests included the Belgian Special Envoy Baron Moncheur, members of his delegation (M. Yturralde, M. Monteyne, M. Anteunis), the Belgian Minister to China (J. Guillaume), the Consul-General (M. Tellefsen), the Vice-Consuls (M. Huboi, M. Delcoigne), the Mayor of Shanghai (Wu Tiecheng), the Secretary-General of the Municipal Government (Tang Shixuan, Li Mo), the Section Chief of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs (Zhao Tiejiang), the President of the Belgian Chamber of Commerce (M. Haelen), the General Manager of the Banque Belge pour l'Étranger (M. Smits), the Manager (M. Lafond), and more than forty others, including Lin Tongshi, Wang Yanxi, and Xie Fusheng.

Welcome Speech

During the banquet, the Chairman of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, Yu Zuoting, delivered the following welcome speech: "Special Envoy Baron Moncheur, bearing the mission of reciprocal visit, has come to China. Since entering the capital and completing the audience with the head of state, he has traveled extensively and visited famous sites in the former capital. Recently, he has returned south from his travels and graced Shanghai with his presence. Our Chamber, as the local host, has prepared a humble feast to welcome the envoy and to express our long-cherished admiration. We are honored by your presence, which makes this gathering even more special. Your country and our country established commercial relations in 1865, which corresponds to the fourth year of the Tongzhi reign in our country. This history is now sixty-nine years old. Although our countries are geographically distant, and few of our citizens engage in commercial activities in your country beyond studying or traveling, your country has left a historically valuable impression on our domestic industrial circles. The earliest railways built in our country, the Guannei Railway (now the Beining Railway) and the Luhan Railway (now the Pinghan Railway), owe much to your country. The latter, which traverses central and northern China, is even more important in terms of transportation than the Guannei Railway. When this railway was initially built, the source of funding and the technical personnel were all borrowed and hired from your country, enabling the completion of this historically significant transportation project in China. We cannot help but express our gratitude for your country's assistance. Furthermore, we have heard that the envoy's visit is associated with an especially memorable story. It is said that the Yellow River Railway Bridge on the Pinghan Railway was designed and built by the envoy's esteemed father when he served as an engineer on that railway. As a Chinese saying goes, 'incense and fire predestined connection.' The envoy's visit to China adds another layer to this relationship, truly demonstrating a profound connection. We also received a letter from our envoy to your country, mentioning that the Special Envoy is also a banker and industrialist, which further enhances the cordial feelings between host and guests at today's gathering. In addition to railways, the Hanyang Iron and Steel Works, the only factory in our country at the time capable of producing steel rails for railways, also employed dozens of engineers and technicians from your country during its initial years of operation. Therefore, although the history of commercial relations between your country and our country may not be as long as that of other countries, it is deeply related to the future of our country's industrial development. This is a source of pride in the history of diplomatic relations between our two countries. Recalling our country's admiration for your country at that time, and our desire to seek your country's assistance in industrial technology, was not only because your country's steel industry was world-renowned, but also because your country, since the Treaty of London in 1831, has been a symbol of world peace, while simultaneously possessing the qualities of determination and decisiveness, respecting the sovereignty of other nations while protecting its own. This aligns perfectly with our country's traditional values, resulting in a seamless spiritual connection and enabling the preservation of valuable memories in our seventy-year diplomatic history. Our association firmly believes that this spirit will continue indefinitely. We wish the Special Envoy good health and a pleasant journey." The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, the Shanghai Banking Association, the Chinese National Federation of Industries, the International Trade Association, and the International Problems Research Association were among the hosts. In response, the Belgian Special Envoy stated, "In my short half-month in your country, I have already witnessed the grandeur of your nation and a glimpse of its great future. Seeing the frugality and hard work of your farmers, I cannot help but feel confident in China's future. As China's industry and commerce flourish, the responsibilities of bankers in national development will undoubtedly be significant." The banquet ended around one o'clock in the afternoon.

The Belgian Minister to China, Mr. Guillaume and his wife, held a grand tea party at the Belgian legation's garden on Route Lafayette yesterday afternoon at 5 p.m., to welcome Special Envoy Johnson and his entire delegation. Attendees included the Special Envoy and his entourage, Minister of Foreign Affairs Wang Zhengting, Vice Minister of Railways Zeng Zhongming, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan Chu Minyi, Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Zhao Jinqing, Yuan Ludeng, Yu Zuoting, Chen Shiguang, Zhao Tiejiang, Wang Liangchun, Xu Peihuang, Zhang Ming, as well as foreign guests such as Italian Minister Possa Grilli and Japanese Minister Ariyoshi Akira, totaling more than 300 people. The Belgian Minister and his wife warmly received the guests with champagne and refreshments. The guests and hosts joyfully dispersed around 7 p.m.

Departure from Shanghai This Morning

Yesterday evening at 8:30 p.m., Mayor Wu hosted a banquet at the Cathay Hotel on the Bund to welcome Special Envoy Johnson and his delegation. The Belgian Minister and his wife, the Belgian Consul-General Mr. Tellefsen and his wife, the Chairman of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Mr. Yu Zuoting, secretaries and directors of the municipal government, and representatives of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs also attended. The banquet concluded around 10 p.m. According to municipal government sources, Special Envoy Johnson is scheduled to depart for his home country on the Italian liner Conte Rosso this morning. The Special Envoy originally planned to board the ship last night, but decided to postpone his departure until 8:30 a.m. this morning due to sufficient time. He will board the Italian liner from the Jianghai Customs Wharf via the customs patrol boat Jinghui. Nine Types of National Bonds, Including Austrian Indemnity Bonds

Principal Repayment Lottery Held Yesterday Morning

A total principal of silver 6,645,000 yuan was repaid.

The 24 Treasury Bonds of the Austrian Indemnity will be paid on the 20th of this month; the remaining will be paid at the end of the month.

According to the Central News Agency, the lottery for the repayment of principal on nine types of national bonds, including the 24 Treasury Bonds of the Austrian Indemnity, was held at 10 a.m. yesterday at the auditorium of the Bankers Association. Representatives from various agencies, organizations, and banks in the city attended to supervise the process. Chiang Lu-fu, the Director of the Public Debt Department of the Ministry of Finance, came to Shanghai to preside over the lottery. Forty-six winning numbers were drawn, with a total principal repayment of silver 6,645,000 yuan. The winning bonds, except for the 24 Treasury Bonds of the Austrian Indemnity, which will be paid with interest starting September 20th by the Central, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications in various locations, will be paid starting September 30th. The details are as follows:

Attending Representatives

Those who attended yesterday morning included Lu Shuping from the Shanghai Municipal Government, Ju Zhijing from the First Special District Court, Liu Wuqiao and Shen Jiuyu from the Money Trade Association, Luo Huizong from the Hankou Chamber of Commerce, Jin Wenyuan from the Central Bank, Chen Zheqing and Zhu Qizhen from the Bank of China, Mao Shijian from the Bank of Communications, Hua Shih Han from the Kuo Hua Bank, Jin Wenwei from the Yung Feng Bank, and Zhou Liangjiang from the Tung Yih Trust Company. Chiang Lu-fu, the director of the Public Debt Department of the Ministry of Finance, was specially dispatched to Shanghai to preside over the event.

Chairman's Report

Principal has already been repaid 18 times, and this is the 19th repayment. Three winning numbers will be drawn, with a principal repayment of silver 450,000 yuan. (4) The Military Supplies Bonds of the Ministry of Finance of the National Government were issued in the 17th year of the Republic of China, with a total value of 10,000,000 yuan. Principal has already been repaid 14 times, and this is the 15th repayment. One winning number will be drawn, with a principal repayment of silver 101,000 yuan. (5) The Short-Term Reconstruction Bonds of the Ministry of Finance of the National Government were issued in the 17th year of the Republic of China, with a total value of 40,000,000 yuan. Principal has already been repaid 17 times, and this is the 18th repayment. Three winning numbers will be drawn, with a principal repayment of silver 1,200,000 yuan. (6) The Short-Term Financial Bonds of the 17th Year of the Republic of China had a total value of 30,000,000 yuan. Principal has already been repaid 11 times, and this is the 12th repayment. (9) The Long-Term Financial Bonds of the 17th Year of the Republic of China were issued in the 17th year of the Republic of China, with a total value of 45,000,000 yuan. Principal has already been repaid once, and this is the second repayment. Twenty-five winning numbers will be drawn, with a principal repayment of silver 1,125,000 yuan. For the above winning bonds, except for the 24 Treasury Bonds of the Austrian Indemnity, which will begin to be paid on September 20th, the remaining eight types of bonds will begin to be paid starting September 30th. The principal and interest payable on all winning bonds will be paid jointly by the Central, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications in various locations. Please have the supervisors verify the drawn numbers and the register of drawn numbers to facilitate the execution of the lottery."

Postal Office to Sell

New Stamp Tax Stamps with Pagoda Design

To be Implemented on November 1st, According to a Proclamation from the Ministry of Finance

The Review Committee of Revenue Collection Agencies to be Terminated in October

The Ministry of Finance has issued a proclamation stating: "The stamp tax is collected on documents and should be based on the principle of actual affixation. All documents subject to stamp tax under the Provisional Regulations on Stamp Tax, except for those of a permanent nature, have a certain period of validity. If merchants and the public can affix stamps as required, the stamps they obtain will be affixed and cancelled on the documents in a timely manner, and the validity of the stamps will expire accordingly. However, in recent years, while many merchants and the public have complied with the regulations, there have also been many who have indulged in bad habits, preferring to pay a fixed amount and not paying attention to actual affixation. Furthermore, revenue collection agencies have sought to simplify matters, indulging in leniency and failing to strictly enforce the regulations. As a result, there has been a backlog of un-affixed stamps in the hands of merchants and the public, which has led to a decline in national tax revenue and, on the merchants' side, often resulted in violations and penalties during strict inspections. This situation, where both the government and the public are in difficulty, calls for urgent remedy. It is hereby stipulated that all provincial stamp tax collection agencies and review committees for cases of violation of stamp tax regulations shall be terminated uniformly by the end of October this year. From November 1st, the Ministry will produce and print new stamp tax stamps with a pagoda design, and entrust them to provincial post offices for sale, so that the public can freely purchase and affix them. In the future, except for the locations designated by the post office for sale, no other agencies or businesses will be allowed to sell them. The responsibility for inspection will be entrusted to the provincial, municipal, and county governments, with personnel from the provincial stamp tax and tobacco and alcohol tax bureaus conducting random inspections. The Ministry will send personnel to supervise the process. Cases of violation of stamp tax laws and regulations will be referred to local judicial organs for handling. The existing old stamp tax stamps can still be used as usual before the end of October. From November 1st, the date the post office begins selling stamps, all documents created must not be affixed with these old stamps, otherwise they will be penalized as if they were not affixed. It should be known that the Ministry is reforming the issuance, inspection, and penalty of stamp tax stamps. The various accumulated malpractices of the past can be cleared up from now on, and merchants and the public will benefit significantly. Furthermore, the revenue from the stamp tax has been designated by the Ministry to be used largely to supplement the reduction of agricultural surtaxes in various provinces. That is, the central government collects more regular tax, and the local government receives more subsidies, which can reduce the surtax by one more share and provide the people with one more share of real benefit. The relationship is even more important. It is hoped that merchants and the public will understand this intention and, from November 1st, purchase stamp tax stamps from the post office and affix them as required for all documents subject to stamp tax. Do not continue to conceal and omit them as before, lest you incur penalties. This proclamation is issued for general knowledge, in addition to submitting it to the relevant departments for implementation. This proclamation is issued on the [blank] day of September in the 23rd year of the Republic of China, by Minister Kong Xiangxi."

Ministry of Finance Restricts Foreign Exchange and Cracks Down on Speculation

Gold and Goods Auctions Suspended Simultaneously Yesterday

The gold market price is standardized according to the London gold bullion price.

It was agreed that swap transactions would be implemented next month, and the market would open today.

The black market rose 15 yuan, resulting in a loss of 30 million yuan.

The Foreign Exchange Committee of the Bank held discussions yesterday.

According to the New Voice News Agency, the Ministry of Finance issued an order the night before last, restricting foreign exchange trading and cracking down on gold speculation. This had a significant impact on banks dealing with foreign exchange and gold exchanges. Yesterday morning, all banks, the Foreign Exchange Committee, and the board of directors of the Gold Exchange held emergency meetings. The Gold Exchange and the Goods Exchange suspended trading for one day. The chairman of the board of directors and the supervisor, Chen Hang, agreed on the standard for gold trading prices, using the Central Bank's London gold bullion price as the benchmark. Subsequently, at the request of the brokerage community, the new standard was postponed to October 15th, when the December contracts roll over. Trading will resume as usual today. Yesterday, the gold black market rose by 15 yuan compared to last Saturday. Details are as follows:

Bank Foreign Exchange Committee Discusses

After receiving the order from the Ministry of Finance, the Bankers Association held a meeting of the Foreign Exchange Committee at 11 a.m. yesterday. Twelve people attended, including Bei Songsun from the Bank of China and Shen Laiqing from the Continental Bank. After detailed discussion, it was reported that their opinions were contributed to the Ministry of Finance, but the content was difficult to disclose. According to one banker, the order from the Ministry of Finance limits foreign exchange trading to three types. However, except for the second item with a clear time frame, the remaining (1 and 3) items, referring to legitimate and normal business and private needs, lack a clear standard, causing those dealing in foreign exchange to be at a loss and forced to stop operations or trade without any transactions. However, foreign banks may not comply with the order, and as a result, it may be a futile attempt to drive away sparrows with scarecrows.

Two Exchanges Suspend Trading for One Day

The Gold Exchange received the order from the Ministry of Finance yesterday through supervisor Chen Hang, prohibiting settlement in foreign exchange and requiring all transactions to be settled in cash. This caused panic among brokers. The chairman of the Brokerage Association, Wang Jiafu, and others requested the chairman of the board of directors, Xu Busun, to temporarily suspend trading for one day. The notice from the board of directors is as follows: "(1) The Shanghai newspapers today contain the order from the Ministry of Finance regarding the exchange. The chairman of the board of directors has already gone to the supervisor's office to seek instructions on how to proceed and should temporarily suspend trading. (2) An emergency meeting will be held at the Gold Trade Association on North Wuxi Road at 2 p.m. today. Please ensure that all brokers are present. (3) Due to the order from the Ministry of Finance, an emergency meeting will be held in the afternoon, allowing trading to be temporarily suspended for one day according to the agreement between the brokers and the association. A further notice will be issued after a decision is made at the meeting." Trading in goods and gold was suspended simultaneously.

Board of Directors Agrees on New Standard

The Gold Exchange held a meeting of the board of directors yesterday morning. Eleven people attended, including Xu Busun, Miao Jinzhi, Cai Jiusheng, Zhao Zhongying, and Wang Zhixiang. The meeting was chaired by Xu Busun, chairman of the board of directors. The following resolutions were made: "(1) Accept the order from the Ministry of Finance prohibiting settlement in foreign exchange. (2) The gold market price has always been standardized according to the US dollar exchange rate. The Ministry of Finance's order does not specify the new standard. After consultation between the chairman of the board of directors and supervisor Chen Jian'an, it was decided to use the Central Bank's daily London gold bullion price as the standard."

Brokers' Association Requests Postponement

At 2 p.m. yesterday, all brokers held a general meeting at the Gold Trade Association on North Wuxi Road, chaired by Deputy Chairman Wang Jiafu, to discuss measures. "(1) Whether to approve the new standard for settlement set by the board of directors." It was resolved that the new standard was difficult to approve. Zhan Liansheng from Hengfengyong Gold Company and Wang Jiafu from Yuanmaoyong Gold Company were elected to negotiate with Chairman Xu Busun. All transactions will temporarily follow the old rules until December this year, and a proper solution will be negotiated. "(2) According to the reports of the two representatives, Chairman Xu Busun was consulted about the new standard, and it was impossible to change it. As for the swap contracts, it may be possible to negotiate a proper solution due to the limited time, or extend it to September 20th or the end of the month." It was resolved that the September 15th October rollover would still follow the old standard, while the October 15th December contracts rollover would all use the new standard. Zhan Liansheng and Wang Jiafu were still nominated to negotiate with the chairman. The two representatives went to see Xu Busun, who then consulted with Supervisor Chen Hang. Only at 4:45 p.m. did Zhan and Wang return to the meeting and report that they had obtained the supervisor's consent. The meeting was then adjourned. Trading will resume as usual this morning. The Exchange has sparked much discussion.

Yesterday, after the Gold Exchange announced a temporary suspension of trading, those who made a living by spreading rumors and scalping went to the exchange to watch and discuss. They said that they would have no place to stand if they could not buy and sell short in the future, because those who made a living by spreading rumors were experienced and had sharp eyes. What they did was foreign exchange. For example, if they bought gold pounds on one side, they would immediately calculate the selling price of francs on the other side. They would make a long position in whichever direction they could profit. If they could not trade in foreign exchange, they would have no way to spread rumors. As for scalping, they watched the market trend and followed the big players to earn small profits. In the future, cracking down on speculation will stabilize the gold price somewhat, and this group of people will have no profit to make.

Gold Black Market Rises 15 Yuan

Although the gold market was closed yesterday, a few firms were still trading. Because there were more short positions in the market, and now that cash trading is required, the short positions are bound to be covered, so the market price soared. The highest price was 965 yuan, and it was said that 77 bars were traded. The smallest price was 58 yuan, and 49 bars were traded. More trades were done at 60 yuan. The last price was around 60 yuan, which was about 15 yuan higher than last Saturday's closing price (949.5 yuan). Due to the gold market's suspension of trading, Chinese merchants poured more than 200,000 pounds of gold into the pound market and more than 1 million US dollars into the US dollar market. The market was extremely chaotic because people were terrified.

Controlling Exchange Rates is Impractical

According to those engaged in international trade, China has always had to bear the responsibility for fluctuations in foreign exchange in addition to the responsibility for price fluctuations of goods in foreign trade. Now, if speculation in gold is prohibited, the price of gold will be more stable, which will reduce the risk for those engaged in international trade. However, because China has extraterritoriality, it can only prohibit Chinese merchants from speculation, but it cannot prohibit foreign merchants from speculation. As a result, gold speculation will be transferred from the hands of Chinese merchants to the hands of foreign merchants, which is actually not helpful to the policy of controlling international exchange rates.

Losses of 30 Million Yuan in One Day

It is also said that because China is a net importer in trade, it is often short in the gold market. Now, it is necessary to trade in cash, so the short positions are bound to be covered, and the gold price is bound to rise further. Taking yesterday's (10th) black market as an example, the total loss to our country in international exchange rates has already exceeded 30 million yuan.

Special Survey Record of Domestic Goods and Industries

(4) Enamel Industry (i.e., Porcelain Enamel Industry)

Enamel is also one of the emerging industries. During the 3rd and 4th years of the Republic of China, enamelware imports exceeded 4 million yuan annually, with Japanese goods accounting for 80%. In the 5th year of the Republic of China, a British businessman named Mr. Macleod established a large factory in Gujiawan, Zhabei, specializing in the production of enamel cups, lunch boxes, and other items. This was the beginning of the enamel industry in Shanghai. Later, Macleod failed to manage the business well and sold it to a Chinese businessman, who reorganized it into the Zhufeng Porcelain Enamel Company. Soon after, the Zhonghua Vocational School opened an enamel department in Lujiabang, with an attached Zhonghua Enamel Factory to provide students with practical training in replicating various utensils. Its reputation rose sharply, and it was subsequently reorganized into a joint-stock company, operating independently and producing its own enamel powder, without the need to rely on imports. As a result, enamel factories were established one after another, with a total of about fourteen or fifteen, with a total capital of 1.17 million yuan, a total of 74 furnaces, and an annual turnover of about 4-5 million yuan. It cannot be said that it does not occupy an important position in the domestic goods industry. Therefore, we visited Mr. Fang Jiange, manager of the Zhonghua Enamel Factory, and Mr. Jin Songtang, a standing committee member of the industry association, to learn about the general situation. The details are recorded below.

The equipment of this industry is complete, and the more scaled manufacturers are Huafeng, Yifeng, Zhonghua Enamel, Jiuxin, and Zhufeng. The existing trade association includes Huafeng, Yifeng, Zhonghua Enamel, Shanghai, Zhufeng, Jiuxin, Xiefeng, and Weiwei. Jiuxin and Shanghai were established in the recent three years. Other manufacturers that have not joined the association are constantly changing. Some have capital of only a few thousand yuan. Last year's turnover was about 4 million yuan, with the Zhonghua factory accounting for more than one-sixth. The production order is divided into five steps: (1) blank making; (2) powder making; (3) blank washing; (4) enameling; (5) art. There are many types of enameled ware, roughly divided into basins, pots, bowls, buckets, shop signs, food baskets, wind stoves, and spittoons. At present, it has become a habit for Chinese people to use domestic goods, so there are very few sales of foreign goods. Last year, enamelware imports within 36 centimeters were less than 100,000 taels, which is gratifying. However, imports of enamelware larger than 36 centimeters still reached hundreds of thousands of taels, which is regrettable. Recently, Japanese enamelware has flooded North China and Southeast Asia, but it has disappeared along the Yangtze River. However, competition among peers is fierce, with price cuts and frequent discounts, which has not happened in ten years. It is heartbreaking to kill each other. If this is not changed, it is feared that it will create opportunities for foreign goods, which is even more frustrating. All raw materials, except for iron sheets that must be imported from the United States, can be produced by various factories. As for the difficulties in the work, it is nothing more than the workers' lack of knowledge, weak skills, and difficulty in producing exquisite products. The working efficiency is not easy to compete with foreigners. In terms of production and sales, Mr. Jin said that there are too few state-run ships (almost none in Southeast Asia), high freight rates, and few railways. Transportation takes time, and it always feels that it cannot be fully developed. Mr. Jin said that except for those who have not joined the association, the factories that have joined the association can maintain their original status and seek development. There is no factory that has failed, but due to insufficient capital, unsound organization, and lack of talent, it always feels difficult to be optimistic. The trend of this industry in the future is to reduce costs, seek outlets widely, and achieve the goal of universal sales. If the factories in the same industry can break the suicidal policy, work together, strive for excellence in technology, avoid unnecessary competition, and avoid arbitrary price cuts, they will be able to drive away foreign goods and make imports disappear. This year, due to the price cuts, the turnover of the same industry in seven months is about 2.5 million yuan, but it is difficult to cope with and difficult to profit. All the colleagues in this factory have only one goal in mind: to strive for perfection in the products and to reduce costs as much as possible, and to make the organization sound and the equipment perfect, so that the future of domestic goods can be developed. Mr. Fang and others have been enthusiastic about promoting domestic goods for decades, studying and investigating tirelessly, and attending exhibitions everywhere. They have also been dedicated to uniting the industry and fighting against foreign countries, which is respectable.

Three Beishangjiang Steamer

Fuhua Propeller Suddenly Damaged

Cargo Transferred by Fuyang Steamer

Returning to Shanghai from Wanxian for Major Repairs

The Three Beishangjiang Steamer Company has a total of two steamers, one named Fuyang and the other named Fuhua. Fuhua was rebuilt from Wuxing and is the best in the Sichuan River line. This time, the steamer was transferring a large number of goods and passengers to Sichuan in Yichang. When it arrived in Wanxian, the steamer's axle suddenly broke, and the engine blades were also suddenly damaged. It was unable to transport goods and passengers to Chongqing and was anchored in Wanxian. It urgently telegraphed the Yichang branch for quick rescue.

Ship Sent to Transfer Cargo

After receiving the telegram, Yichang Branch Manager Ren Ziqing immediately dispatched the Fuyang steamer to Wanxian to transfer all the cargo and passengers from the Fuhua steamer to Chongqing. Yesterday, news came from Yichang that the cargo and passengers from the Fuhua steamer had been transferred to the Fuyang steamer on the 6th of this month and would be unloaded in Chongqing soon.

Returning to Shanghai for Repairs

The Shanghai head office telegraphed the steamer to return to Shanghai and quickly enter the factory for repairs, replacing the axle and installing new engine blades. According to the telegram, the steamer will sail down from Wanxian today and return to Shanghai for major repairs. It is also reported that the steamer is still equipped with a single blade and is returning to Shanghai empty. It may be able to sail on its own without the need for a ship to tow it.

Qinghai Princes

Ya Qingqi Arrives in Xiamen Together

To Investigate Education and Industry

Xiamen Correspondence: Qinghai Princes Ya Qingqi, under the order of the twenty-nine banners of Qinghai, investigate the state of domestic education, industry, and technology in order to learn from it to improve Qinghai's education and industry. Ya first took his post, passing through Gansu, Hebei, Shanxi, Shandong, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Guangdong, Guangxi, and other provinces. A few days ago, he arrived in Xiamen with Li Zimao, the commander of the Seventh Security Region, and Huang Jianzhong, the general director of the Shanghai Overseas Chinese Federation, and stayed at the Tianxian Hotel. He inspected the facilities of Xiamen University and Jimei School, visited Lin Wenqing, the president of Xiamen University, and Hong Hongru, the president of the Chamber of Commerce. A welcome meeting was held by various parties at the Daxia Hotel on the 3rd. Ya hoped that the country would quickly become prosperous and strong, and consolidate national defense to resist foreign aggression. He also attended a banquet hosted by the International Rotary Club on the 6th. During the banquet, Ya recounted the historical evolution of the Mongolian people, explained the awakening of the Mongolian people, and their recent rapprochement with the central government, demonstrating the spirit of Chinese national unity. Finally, he said that he had come under the order of the leader of the twenty-ninth tribe of Qinghai to investigate the progress of education, industry, and technology in various provinces, preparing to be the forerunner for the development of Qinghai. (7th)

International Commercial Telegraph

– September 10th, Reuters Special Commercial News –

Gold and Silver: London Gold Price: This morning's gold price was 140 shillings and 11.5 pence, 2.5 pence higher than Saturday's price.

London Silver: In today's silver market, purchases by the United States, India, and speculators were not enough to offset sales by China, so the price fell slightly. The spot price is 21 pence and 8125, and the futures price is 21 pence and 875, both down 0625. The market is stable.

Bombay Silver: Today's silver market is stable. The spot price is 60 rupees and 8 annas, the October price is 60 rupees and 9 annas, and the November price is 60 rupees and 11 annas, all up 3 annas.

Exchange Rates:

British-American: In the London foreign exchange market, the British-American exchange rate opened at 5.00125 yuan, down 125 from Saturday's closing price. At noon, it fell 5625 to 4.995625 yuan. The market then became quiet, and finally rose 375 to 4.999375 yuan. Also, one US dollar equals 4 shillings and 007 British gold.

British-French: This morning's opening price was 74 francs and 90, 3 pounds higher than Saturday's closing price. At 11:00, it fell 6 pounds to 74 francs and 84. The market then became sluggish until 2:00 p.m., when it began to change, rebounding 6 pounds to 74 francs and 90, the same as the opening price.

American-British: The New York foreign exchange market was quiet this morning. The American-British exchange rate opened at 4.99625 yuan, down 615. At 10:30, the price rebounded 125 to 4.99575 yuan.

Cotton and Wheat:

American Cotton: The US Department of Agriculture's cotton production report was favorable to the short side, so the cotton market opened today with more sellers and the price fell by about 24 pounds. However, demand was good and absorbed the selling, and the price rebounded by 7 pounds. At 10:40, it fell another 1 pound.

Indian Cotton: Bombay Cotton Market: The price fell initially today due to large-scale liquidations by multiple parties and speculative selling. It then rose due to low-priced purchases by European export businesses. The April-May Balochistan cotton price was 221 rupees, up 1 rupee and 25.

British Cotton: Liverpool Cotton Market: Prices fell sharply due to the release of the US Department of Agriculture's cotton production report. At 1:00 p.m., the October price was 6.86, 18 pounds lower than Saturday's closing price.

British Wheat: Liverpool Wheat Market: The price fell this morning. At 1:00 p.m., the October price was 5 yuan and 9 pence, down 1 penny.

American Wheat: The wheat market opened about 275 lower, falling with other commodities. However, it is expected that the government's grain report will be favorable to the long side, so the market price strengthened before noon, rising 15 at 10:40.

Rubber:

London: This morning's market was stable. At noon, the成交 price for January was 7 pence and 6875, the same as Friday's closing price.

New York: The rubber market opened with the price down 56 pounds, and then fell another 5 pounds. However, futures were still stable. At 10:40, the market price had not changed.

As soon as prices rise, buying interest stops immediately. When the securities market opened this morning, the market was quiet and stable. The prices of various securities fell slightly. Local News 6

Belgian Envoy on a Reciprocal Visit

Johnson Arrived in Shanghai from Beijing Yesterday

Mayor Wu and Others Personally Welcomed Him in a Grand Ceremony

Five Major Groups Including the Municipal Chamber of Commerce Gave a Public Banquet Yesterday Afternoon

The Envoy and His Party Are Scheduled to Depart for Their Country This Morning

Baron Johnson, the special envoy sent by Belgium on a reciprocal visit to China, paid his respects to President Lin of the National Government in Beijing on the morning of the 8th, and visited Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Mausoleum. He then took the night train with a private railway car attached to Shanghai the night before. He arrived at the North Station at 7:40 a.m. yesterday. Belgian Ambassador Ji Youmu and the envoy's secretaries and attendants also came along. Mayor Wu and others personally welcomed him in a grand ceremony. At noon, he attended a banquet hosted by various groups. In the afternoon, the Belgian ambassador held a tea party. In the evening, Mayor Wu hosted a banquet. The Belgian envoy was originally scheduled to board the Italian ship Conte Rosso that night, but it has now been decided that he will board the ship and return to his country at 8:30 a.m. this morning. The details are as follows:

Enthusiastic Welcome

At the entrance of the North Station, the national flags of China and Belgium were hung high yesterday morning. The area around the station and the area around Jielu and Baoshan Road were guarded by armed police officers dispatched by the Public Security Bureau. Inside the station and on the platform, railway police officers and security team soldiers were on guard with live ammunition. The 120-member honor guard of the Municipal Security Office and the military band of the Public Security Bureau were lined up at the front of the platform, playing music to welcome the envoy. All welcomers entered the station with temporary yellow cloth passes issued in advance by the Municipal Government. Security was tight and order was maintained. Those who went to welcome the envoy included Mayor Wu, Luo Weixiong, the chief of the staff office of the Garrison Headquarters, Gan, Staff Officer Wu, Fan Wei, Tang Tuxuan, Geng Jiaji, and Zhang Tingrong, secretaries of the Municipal Government, Zhao Tiehan, the acting director of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Yang Hu, the director of the Security Office, Wang Chengzhi, a secretary, Wen Hong'en, the director of the Public Security Bureau, Li Hongqi, a secretary, Wu Shaozeng, the deputy director of the two roads, Tan Erfu, the Belgian Consul General, Hu Bieyi, the consul, De Er'ai, the vice consul, Bart, the counselor, Shi Mengzi, the general manager of Wah Bi Bank, Hayes, the president of the Belgian Chamber of Commerce, and Maurice, and representatives from various circles in China and Belgium, more than 60 people.

Arrival

The Belgian envoy and his party arrived in Shanghai the night before on a specially prepared railway car attached to the Beijing-Shanghai train. The car arrived at the North Station at 7:40 a.m. yesterday. After the private railway car entered the platform, the military band of the Public Security Bureau played the Belgian national anthem and a welcome song. Belgian Envoy Johnson and Belgian Ambassador Ji Youmu and others got off the train amidst the melodious sound of military music, shook hands with the welcoming personnel one by one, and exchanged pleasantries briefly. Mayor Wu and others accompanied them out of the platform to the front of the station gate. Johnson and his wife rode in the Municipal Government car parked in front of the gate to the Cathay Hotel on the Bund to rest. Belgian Ambassador Ji Youmu and others rode in the Municipal Government cars following behind. All the welcoming cars had the national flags of China and Belgium hanging on the front. The mayor accompanied the Belgian envoy to the Cathay Hotel residence. After a brief conversation, he bid farewell.

Companions

Those who came with Belgian Envoy Baron Johnson and his wife yesterday morning included Belgian Ambassador Ji Youmu and his wife, the envoy's counselor Ye Tu and his wife, Secretary Hailmens, Johnson Company's Ander Johnson, Military Attache Monte Ang, and Lin Tongshi, the special commissioner of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Liaison Department, and Secretary Wang Yanxi, who took care of them on the train. Chu Minyi, the secretary-general of the Executive Yuan, also accompanied them to Shanghai.

Visit to the Mayor

After resting briefly at the Cathay Hotel, the special delegation, together with Belgian Ambassador Ji Youmu, took a car to the Municipal Government in the city center to visit Mayor Wu at about 10:00 a.m. When the car arrived at the Municipal Government, the military band of the Public Security Bureau stationed in front of the Municipal Government played music to welcome them. At the same time, the police and honor guards of the Security Office and the Public Security Bureau who were guarding the Municipal Government also saluted with their guns. The special delegation and the Belgian ambassador got out of the car amidst the melodious sound of military music. Mayor Wu personally led Secretary-General Yu Hongjun, English Secretary Tang Shixuan, and French Secretary Geng Jiaji to the mayor's reception room for a conversation of more than ten minutes. The special delegation then bid farewell to the Belgian ambassador, and the mayor sent them off as usual. Secretary Tang accompanied them back to the special envoy's residence at the Cathay Hotel. Mayor Wu, accompanied by Secretary-General Yu Hongjun, Security Office Director Yang Hu, and Secretaries Tang Shixuan and Geng Jiaji, took a car to the Cathay Hotel to return the visit at 12:00 noon. The Belgian envoy, the Belgian ambassador, and all the members of the delegation received them in the reception room downstairs of the hotel and had a conversation of more than twenty minutes. Mayor Wu then bid farewell to everyone, and the Belgian envoy sent them off as usual.

Public Banquet

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Banking Association, the General Federation of Industries, the International Trade Association, the International Problems Research Association, and other five groups held a public banquet at the Hong Kong Road Bank Club at noon yesterday.

Commercial News 7

Finance

Gold Exchange Temporarily Suspended Yesterday

Business as Usual Today

New Transactions Based on London Gold Bullion Settlement Price

Unexpired Swap Transactions Settled According to Original Methods

The Gold Exchange suspended trading yesterday due to an order from the Ministry of Finance to crack down on speculative activities. All new transactions must be settled in cash, and foreign exchange settlements are prohibited. This sudden development caused considerable confusion in the market. The board of directors issued a brief temporary notice before the market opened and later issued the following announcement: "Due to the Ministry of Finance's order, an emergency meeting will be held this afternoon. Brokers are allowed to negotiate with the Exchange to suspend trading for one day. A further announcement will be made after the meeting's decision." According to the latest news, the Gold Trade Association has decided that new transactions will be settled based on the London gold bullion price, effective October 15th. Existing swap transactions will be settled according to the original methods. Therefore, the gold market is expected to resume business as usual today (the 11th).

Cash Settlement Required

Gold Market "Gray Market" Soars

Ministry of Finance Cracks Down on Foreign Exchange Draft Speculation

U.S. Considers Banning Private Silver Imports

Due to the Ministry of Finance's order cracking down on gold margin foreign exchange speculation (intended to prevent the outflow of cash), all new transactions must be settled in cash. This news led the Gold Exchange to fear an unexpected price surge and decided to suspend trading for one day, pending an emergency meeting to determine the course of action. However, the "gray market" within the exchange remained relatively active, although the number of transactions was naturally small. The initial announcement of the Ministry of Finance's order to stop foreign exchange speculation, coupled with the news that new transactions must be settled in cash, greatly boosted market sentiment. Furthermore, the U.S. Treasury's intention to ban private silver imports dealt a significant blow to short sellers, causing widespread panic. However, due to the market suspension, there was no standard price. Nevertheless, the "gray market" saw transactions at 970 yuan due to the extreme tightness of the foreign exchange market. Later, HSBC quoted a reduction of 1.25 for Sterling and 0.25 for USD. After the announcement, the internal market shifted from tight to loose, with sellers appearing at 65 yuan. Mitsui offered December USD at 31.25, retreating to within 60 yuan. Generally, Western merchants showed selling interest, with transactions at 958 yuan. Afterwards, the "gray market" gradually became public, with some trading activity, struggling around the 60 yuan mark. Near noon, transactions surged slightly, with some buying hundreds of bars at 60 yuan. However, sellers were also eager, making it difficult to rise to 61 yuan, although the underlying sentiment remained firm. There were no legitimate transactions in the later market, but some small deals outside the door were priced at slightly above 60 yuan. The USD settlement price today was 992 yuan due to HSBC's quoted reduction of 0.25, which is equivalent to a margin price. Calculated based on a margin price of 960 yuan, the "button" [discount or premium] was approximately 32 yuan, 8 yuan less than last Saturday. In this urgent and changing situation, the Gold Exchange had no choice but to convene an emergency meeting at the Gold Trade Association at 2 PM. It is rumored that the new standard will be changed to Customs Gold settlement. The calculation method is to multiply Customs Gold by 508. Today, Customs Gold was quoted at 19.13, resulting in a settlement price of 977 yuan.

Chinese Merchants Forced to Cover Shorts

Sudden Tightening of Foreign Exchange

According to yesterday's foreign dispatches, London's large amounts increased by 0.0625 for both near and far terms, while the U.S. bank remained unchanged. London spot gold decreased by half a penny, Sterling increased by 0.0375 against the USD, the USD increased by 0.025 against Sterling, and Sterling increased by 9 pounds against the French franc, while the USD against the French franc remained unchanged. Reports stated that the Ministry of Finance ordered a crackdown on gold margin foreign exchange speculation, causing Chinese merchants to urgently cover their short positions. In addition, reports indicated that the U.S. Treasury Department intends to prohibit the import of private silver. Historically, this port's drafts have been resold by various banks from silver. If this becomes a reality, the export of silver should be undertaken by an official mechanism, and the foreign exchange market will lack large positions, which is not conducive to short positions. Therefore, the informal foreign exchange market opened this morning with a bid price of 1 shilling, 5 pence and 0.125 for Sterling and 35.5625 yuan for USD. Chinese merchants, such as Yu Qingyong, tried hard to cover their positions, but banks lacked selling interest, and brokers refused to help Chinese merchants exit. In an instant, there was an extreme tightening. December USD approached 35, and Sterling actually retreated to within 5 pence. After the HSBC listing was announced, Sterling decreased by 0.125 and USD decreased by 0.25. Banks were willing to sell, and Chinese merchants were exhausted. Consequently, the market gradually hardened, with slight swaps in Sterling. The noon close price for Sterling was 1 shilling, 4 pence and 0.875, and for USD, 35.25 yuan. Later, trading became even thinner, with Chinese merchants still covering. Bombay rose by 1.12 anna, and the domestic market loosened slightly. As transactions were already few, Bombay reported no movement. Finally, the market was mediocre. The closing price for the near-term Sterling was 1 shilling, 4 pence and 0.9375, and for the USD, 35.25 yuan. Compared to last Saturday, Sterling tightened by 0.1875 and USD tightened by 0.4375. Chinese merchants covered approximately 1.5 million USD and nearly 100,000 pounds in Sterling. The overall situation was chaotic. The day's transactions are recorded below:

Sterling opened this morning with a near-term bid price of 1 shilling, 5 pence and 0.125. After opening, the market tightened immediately. MacGregor covered December at 5 pence. Central sold to MacGregor September at 5 pence. MacGregor covered October at the same price. HSBC covered December at the same price. Great Britain benefited from covering December at 0.9375 and October at 0.875. Beneficial covering January at 0.0625 and selling December at 5 pence. The noon close price for Sterling was 1 shilling, 4 pence and 0.9375. In the later market, Citibank covered November at 0.9375. Anda sold to Huabi October at 0.935. The closing selling price ranged from 1 shilling, 4 pence and 0.9375 to 1 shilling, 5 pence, with the buying price increased by 0.0625.

USD opened this morning with a near-term bid price of 35.5625 yuan or 0.625. MacGregor covered October at 0.5. Huabi covered December at 0.5. Citibank covered the same month at 0.375. Great Britain covered the same month at 0.25. Huabi Citibank covered the same month at 0.1875. MacGregor covered the same month at 0.125 and 0.625. Zhejiang Korea Huabi covered December at 0.25. Weekly Interbank Rate Returns to One Cent

The silver dollar market situation: Due to the bank holiday on the previous Sunday, there were various unresolved procedures that needed to be completed yesterday, resulting in a lively market atmosphere, which was more active than in the previous few days. The interbank lending rate was the same in both the morning and afternoon markets at one cent, which was one point higher than the previous day. The additional interest charge (劃頭加水) initially started at two points and then changed to four points, which was also a significant improvement. In terms of interbank loan transactions, the morning market saw over 4.7 million in fund transfers and new transactions, while the afternoon market saw over 200,000 in transactions. Transactions in the Small General Association totaled over 400,000. Silver pawn transactions saw redemptions of over 900,000 and new loans of over 1.4 million. In terms of bank receipts and payments, foreign banks received over 3.1 million in checks and drafts, over 700,000 in telegraphic transfers, over 2.5 million in foreign exchange settlements, and over 4.3 million in various goods and foreign exchange collateral and miscellaneous receipts, with 600,000 in warehouse releases. Chinese banks received over 3.9 million in checks and drafts, over 700,000 in telegraphic transfers, over 800,000 in customs duties, over 1.8 million in foreign exchange settlements, and over 5.8 million in various foreign exchange goods collateral and miscellaneous receipts, with 500,000 in warehouse entries. Japanese banks received over 2.6 million in checks and drafts, over 3.4 million in foreign exchange settlements, and over 5.2 million in various foreign exchange goods collateral and miscellaneous receipts, with 700,000 in warehouse releases. Money shops' silver public bills receipts totaled over 41.1 million, receipts from additional interest charges (洋劃頭欵) totaled over 7.4 million, banknote withdrawals totaled over 1.2 million, issuance totaled over 1.5 million, cash receipts totaled over 800,000, remittances from various regions totaled over 700,000, customer funds totaled 200,000, and payments totaled 350,000. Furthermore, the total amount exchanged at the local clearing house was 16,656,810.70 silver dollars, including 5,229,6509.66 silver dollars and 11,427,1601.04 silver dollars in exchange clearing.

Jiangnan Small Dollars and Copper Coins Rebound

After falling at the beginning of the month, Jiangnan small dollars remained stagnant for five or six days. Yesterday, the market saw slightly brisk trading, and prices also increased. The morning market increased by 0.50 yuan, trading at 833.50 yuan. The afternoon market continued to increase by 1.50 yuan, trading at 835 yuan. Therefore, the result was an increase of 2 yuan compared to the previous day, with 4,000 角 traded in the morning market and 7,000 角 traded in the afternoon market. Guangdong small dollars were slightly lower. The morning and afternoon markets were both at 748.70 yuan, which was 0.06 yuan lower than the previous day. A total of 105,000 角 was traded in the morning market and 25,000 角 was traded in the afternoon market. Copper coins, after some people manipulated the market and prices fell, finally saw a rebound yesterday, trading at 320,000 文, which was 3,000 文 higher than the previous day. The trading value was 13,000 yuan, equivalent to 41,600 串文.

Securities

Public Bonds Experienced a Sudden Decline in Both Rounds

Resulting in Drops Ranging from 0.02, 0.03 to 1.20 Yuan

Yesterday, the market at the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange was extremely peaceful, and the environment was stable. The interbank lending rate was fixed. However, rumors suddenly spread that a certain party had sent a telegram, which was fueled by short sellers on the floor, who took the opportunity to pressure the market, causing an unnecessary decline. Afterwards, the market returned to peace. The rapid changes inevitably led to criticism of self-inflicted panic. Based on the current situation, the market should continue to fluctuate upwards, as buying interest was seen in the No. 46 issue, and selling interest in the No. 4 issue was scarce. Short sellers on the floor are about to cover their positions. Yesterday's performance: The market opened with a uniform upward trend, with most issues increasing by 0.05, 0.10 to about 0.50 yuan. However, the gains in the following issues were slightly weaker. In the second round, rumors suddenly spread, and the decline became more severe, with some issues falling by as much as 1.20 yuan. In the evening, the earlier issues caught up with the decline, with Troop Reduction falling by about 1 yuan. However, the market gradually stabilized, and the distant maturities of the Consolidated Tax issue were slightly better by 0.05. Yarn and Cloth

Coarse Yarn Sales to Guangdong Are Booming

Standard Yarn Reaches New Low

The actual sales of cotton yarn are noticeably improving. Demand from the southern ports is quite robust. There is a rumor that Guangzhou will increase import duties on cotton yarn starting October 1st (whether this is true remains to be proven). Therefore, those buyers are taking precautions and buying over a thousand bales in advance. However, market sentiment remains difficult to excite. The fact that the market price has fallen by 1 yuan despite brisk yarn sales shows how deeply entrenched the market's problems are.

Golden Rooster Japanese Mills Liquidating Distant Futures

At the opening of the margin yarn market, the increased U.S. cotton production figures dampened market sentiment, causing all months to reach new lows. Later, as actual yarn sales were relatively brisk, prices rose slightly in the second and third rounds. The result was a drop of 0.03, 0.04, 0.07, 0.08 yuan for all months. It was rumored that Japanese mills were liquidating distant futures. The market remained flat in the afternoon. In the second round, the market showed signs of vigor, with buyers from Guangdong and Yunnan purchasing 1,500-1,600 bales of spot yarn. Other buyers also made transactions, totaling over 2,500 bales. However, prices fell again in the distant months at the close of the market. This was because the buyers were mainly buying coarse yarn, and sales of 20-count yarn remained weak. The result was an increase of 0.02 yuan in the near months and a drop of 0.01, 0.02, 0.03 yuan in the distant months. The total trading volume for the day was 47,100 bales. Cotton Market Trend Weakening

The cotton market is trending downwards, and the situation is weakening daily. Although everyone predicted that the second estimate of U.S. cotton production would be reduced, the published figure actually increased by 57,000 bales, which greatly disappointed bullish investors. However, buyers are still not loosening their grip, and the price decline is not severe. Yesterday, over 3,000 bales of Yao cotton arrived, with opening prices falling by 1.20 to 1.40 yuan. If the sources of cotton continue to arrive in large quantities, the situation in the cotton market cannot be predicted.

Margin Cotton Falls Again by 0.02-0.03 Yuan

At the opening of the margin cotton market, the increased U.S. cotton production estimate disappointed bullish investors. According to private telegrams, U.S. cotton prices fell by 20-30 pounds after the USDA released its production figures. Therefore, market sentiment was already weak at the opening, with prices falling by 0.02-0.03 yuan in all months. At the same time, it was rumored that over 3,000 bales of Yao cotton had arrived, with opening prices falling sharply by 1.24 yuan. However, one speculator purchased over 7,000 dan, causing prices to rebound. The result was a fall of 0.03 yuan in October and 0.01-0.02 yuan in the distant months. The market was flat at the afternoon opening, and prices fell again at the close. The result was a fall of 0.05-0.10 yuan in all months. The total trading volume for the day was 123,900 dan.
